text1;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》是维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">同时，鉴于</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">中国人权捍卫者（<span lang="EN-US">CHRD</span>）</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">所属的</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库</span></b></span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">已将本网月度报告中所涉及的良心犯均全部收录，因此，我们从<span lang="EN-US">101</span>期起，将绝大多数本月没有动态信息的良心犯简历不再在月度报告里显示。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">我们仍将把在押良心犯名录附于报告内，读者可以根据姓名登录进入《中国大陆良心犯数据库》</span></span></span><a href="https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://tenchu.org/pocd/public/</span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">查询所有相关信息，非常便捷。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">《中国大陆良心犯数据库》不但收录了目前在押的这个良心犯、政治犯，已经获释、死亡的良心犯、政治犯也在此数据库中可以查询到。《中国大陆良心犯数据库》收集工作整理自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月开始，截至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日共 收录良心犯资料共<span lang="EN-US">3571</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯——这里包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集、撰写和编辑，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本报告为了便于人们查询检索，完全以良心犯、政治犯的姓名拼音顺序制作了完整的在押人员名录。同时，本报告仍对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、缓刑或刑满释放，都将从报告正式在押名单中移除，但其简历将显示于本期报告中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本报告每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">9</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">年来，本网一共收集、整理、编辑过的有较为翔实资料的人员名单及其简历超过<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多个<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">九年多如一日，本网持续不断地对中国大陆政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议谴责中共当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对良心犯政治犯施加酷刑，而在中共狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网坚信，外界坚持不懈的关注，将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助！本报告一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">以此</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">九年多的风风雨雨已经过去，未来的道路上还会有千难万险，但是有你们的支持，我们仍将一如既往勇往直前！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">最后，本报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，报告所反映的只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">如发现纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请指正，并尽可能知会本网。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本网邮箱：</span></b></span></span><a href="mailto:wqw2011@gmail.com"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoListParagraph" style="margin-left: 36.0pt; mso-char-indent-count: 0; mso-list: l14 level1 lfo24; text-indent: -36.0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><!--[if !supportLists]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"><span style="mso-list: Ignore;">一、<span style="font: 7.0pt &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><!--[endif]--><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本期报告概述：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。此为第<span lang="EN-US">111</span>期。至此，本报告月月发布历时已整整九年多。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">本期报告全文共计</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">五万六千字</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">。本期报告对上期报告的所有政治犯、良心犯名单进行了一次全面的逐一核查。获悉上期名单中</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">44</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">人已被</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">刑满释放或取保获释。本期获悉有<span lang="EN-US">2</span>名良心犯在狱中被迫害致死。并获悉有被羁押的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人狱中有新动态，</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">同时，本期新增了我们又搜集的被刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">/</span>被精神病<span lang="EN-US">/</span>强迫失踪的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人以及被判刑的<span lang="EN-US">38</span>人，合计<span lang="EN-US">41</span>人的名单及简介。目前，被本期报告录入姓名发布的在押良心犯、政治犯共</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">1651</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">为便于人们查询，《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为本报告名单的唯一索引。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。同时，本报告对所有良心犯、政治犯的刑期进行了统计，羁押未判的也全部列于最后。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><a _Hlk175727158;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></a></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162449568;"></span><span style="mso-bookmark: mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">金永新、靳玉玲、景润茹、寇爱梅、李萍、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、白彦宾：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">内蒙古赤峰市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生，赤峰市喀喇沁旗王爷府镇下瓦房村人。自中共一九九九年七月发动对法轮功的疯狂迫害后，白彦宾多次遭到中共人员的骚扰、抄家、抓捕、关押、被迫流离失所，他家人曾经七年不能团圆。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午，白彦宾发法轮功资料被国保监控发现，白彦宾被喀喇沁旗国保大队警察抓捕，警察抄走他家中的电脑、摩托车等私人物品及现金一万多元，将他关押在喀喇沁旗锦山看守所，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日强迫他交三千元取保候审，并且要他每周一次去喀喇沁旗锦山镇派出所签到。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，喀喇沁旗检察院将白彦宾起诉到喀喇沁旗法院。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，喀喇沁旗公安局警察将其拘留，将他关押到喀喇沁旗看守所。内蒙古赤峰市喀喇沁旗法院于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日对法轮功学员白彦宾判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一千元，并将他关押到赤峰市第四监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span mso-themecolor: text1;">宁夏中卫市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年出生，个体工商户，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日因控告江泽民，被中卫市公安局沙坡头分局行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被中卫市公安局沙坡头分局警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、<a name="_Hlk186272751">陈淑琴</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">宁夏固原市隆德县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，大专文化，内科主治医师，系原隆德县医院医生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日下午，陈淑琴给路人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>份法轮功资料让他去了解，不料被此人恶告，随后被城关派出所两个警察抓捕。隆德国保大队王胜强带人抄家及到单位搜查，抢走所有大法书籍，笔记本计算机等部份私人物品。陈淑琴当时被王胜强等人抓捕到固原市看守所，看守所拒收。国保人员给陈淑琴办了取保候审。陈淑琴回家并正常上班，大约在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月中旬突然失踪。后获悉，陈淑琴又被抓捕、批捕。陈淑琴被关押在宁夏固原市看守所。后获悉，陈淑琴医生，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，已被关押到宁夏女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">5</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">、杜志俊：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">四川省绵阳市江油市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁。杜志俊、吴启慧夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被江油市公安局国保大队抄家，抢走电脑和所有大法书籍并被抓捕。杜志俊被抓捕到江油市看守所，吴启慧被抓捕到绵阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，杜志俊被江油市法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半；吴启慧被江油市法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/17/445046.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">6</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、范一平：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1950</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年代生，广东省广州市人，中共干部家庭出身，曾就读于军医大学，毕业后任外科医生，后转行成为某食品贸易公司经营者，成功珠宝商，自民主墙以来的老民运，中国在押政治犯。自民主墙时期就参与民主运动，多年来一直致力于推动中国社会的人权及法治进步事业，故长期受到当局监控和敏感时期被限制人身自由；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年末，曾因接待秘密回国推动民主运动的中国异议人士王炳章，并帮助另一位异见人士王希哲逃往美国，而被中共广东当局判刑入狱三年；出狱后，因继续持守民主理念和抗争，<span lang="EN-US"> 2014</span>年六四前夕，曾再次被广州警方以“寻衅滋事” 为由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，其居所遭搜查；因中共最高领导人习近平主政以来，对民主异见人士监控、打压愈加强烈，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其与另四名民运人士范文成、赖见君、乔连红、韦亚妮在“广州<span lang="EN-US">11</span>·<span lang="EN-US">12</span>大抓捕”中，被广州市警方先后以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”抄家后带走；次日，其被送进医院，而后被指定居所监视住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，除乔连红被取保释放之外，其与接续被抓捕的赖天龙及范文成、胡天峰等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人均被广州市国家安全局以同罪名正式批捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人案被当地警方移交至广州市检察院审查起诉，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其案件又被移送到广州市中级法院；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人均被以“颠覆国家政权罪”起诉，案由涉及组党，具体事实多为聚餐闲聊时政、去云南旅游等；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人案被广州市检察院移交至广州市中级法院；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，终被广州市中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。目前被羁押于广州巿花都看守所（广东省广州市花都区新华镇宝华路<span lang="EN-US">32</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">510899</span>）。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/11124.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份左右，何庆云被郑州市新郑法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span text1;">、胡德元：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span mso-themecolor: text1;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1944</span>年生，江西省鹰潭市法轮功学员。胡德元为原鹰潭市铁路公安人员，后因坚持修炼法轮功，被开除公职。他曾经多次被劳教、关押，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被判刑。第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被枉判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日发放法轮功资料，被警察抓捕、刑拘、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获悉他已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b name="_Hlk186273004">黄爱华</a>：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，广东省揭阳市榕城区梅云镇人，她与丈夫长期在广东东莞做生意。黄爱华利用做生意之便，向顾客讲法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，黄爱华遭东莞市警察抄家，被抢走大法书籍等财物，并被抓捕到东莞市看守所关押。后得知，黄爱华已经被东莞法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。目前她仍被关押在东莞市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/20/441229.html</span></u><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">、江笑容：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span text1;">四川省德阳市法轮功学员，女，家住德阳市旌阳区八角井街道（原八角井镇）。江笑容女士因宣传法轮功，遭两个不明真相的小学生举报，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被德阳市公安局旌阳分局工农村派出所所谓“专案组”警察入室抓捕、构陷。随即被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，她被德阳市旌阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">8</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年金永新在山东省监狱十一监区遭严管、关禁闭等迫害。金永新被打成脑中风、脑血栓、血压高达<span lang="EN-US">260</span>，被送去医院住院抢救，留下后遗症，手脚不灵活，走路缓慢。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日法轮功学员白玉珍、靳玉玲被信阳市警察入室抓捕，后被构陷至信阳市潢川县检察院、法院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁，进法庭时，身体走路都不稳。在开庭过程中，靳玉玲、白玉珍一直还被强制戴着手铐。靳玉玲被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；白玉珍被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，景润茹被关押到黑龙江省哈尔滨女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">陕西宝鸡石油机械厂法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，宝鸡市金台公安分局出动了多辆警车、几十个警察，抓捕了宝鸡石油机械厂的八名法轮功学员及家属。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，秦丽杰、李宝莲、寇爱梅三人被关押到宝鸡第二看守所非法逮捕、关押，其他人已于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被释放回家。后获悉秦丽杰被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，寇爱梅被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，李宝莲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。寇爱梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; lang="EN-US">12</span>名凌源市法轮功学员。栗静是其中之一，栗静被关押在朝阳市女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日、<span text1;">：黑龙江大庆市杜蒙县法轮功学员。一九六三年九月九日出生，今年五十九岁，蒙族，是下岗民办教师，现住黑龙江省大庆市杜蒙县。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年开始修炼法轮功。因为坚持修炼法轮大法，在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年期间，刘淑萍几次被大庆市局国保和杜蒙县国保便衣警察抓捕，将她构陷到让胡路区检察院、让胡路区法院，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b text1;">、刘嗣祖：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">宁夏银川市隆德县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生。刘嗣祖因坚持法轮信仰，多年来遭到中共人员的各种迫害：他曾两次被中共法院判刑：<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被隆德县法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年缓刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被银川市兴庆区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日下午，刘嗣祖在外出时被警察抓捕，随后派出所警察和国保人员闯到他家中抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月下旬，刘嗣祖被银川市兴庆区公安局构陷到银川市西夏区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月中旬，传出刘嗣祖被银川市西夏区法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。娄亚红上诉后，被中级法院维持原判。如今，娄亚红已被投入新乡女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: lang="EN-US">6</span>合庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，马庆霞开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日晚上<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多钟，马庆霞家来了<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个警察，抄家，抄走大法书籍、两台计算机、真相币、墙上的壁画和<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万多元钱等私人物品，并让马庆霞签字，马庆霞没有配合警察的要求，没有签字。警察将马庆霞抓捕到黄庄派出所，第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，转到刑警队关押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日得知，被在看守所的马庆霞遭批捕。现得知，马庆霞被武清区法院被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，被劫入天津女子监狱，被关押在<span lang="EN-US">9</span>监区。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，任桂芬和丈夫李洪军，及姐姐任桂娥和妹妹遭本溪市明山区公安分局、卧龙派出所警察抓捕。妹妹随后回家。任桂芬和姐姐任桂娥被关押到本溪看守所。任桂芬后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，她被关押到辽宁省女子监狱，现被关押在十二监区（即集训矫治监区）。辽宁省女子监狱通知家属，称不许存钱、接见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span text1;">、王红：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">西安市鄠邑区法轮功女学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生。法轮功女学员王红、董玉英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在鄠邑区将村镇附近讲真相时，被人恶意举报，被将村镇派出所警察抓捕，关押在西安市莲湖区看守所。王红因检查身体不适，被放回家。两人都被构陷到检察院、法院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月西安市莲湖区法院非法庭审两名法轮功学员，王红坚持自己无罪，为自己做了有理有据的无罪辩护。王红保外就医在家，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日王红被蒋村镇派出所与鄠邑区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>警察在家绑架，现在被非法关押在西安市莲湖区看守所。后王红被西安市莲湖区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日止。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/8/27/2021-8-27.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、王卫真：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span mso-themecolor: text1;">大连法轮功学员、女、原沈阳军区大连高等医学专科学校内科教研室任教员，授衔上校，副师待遇。因坚持信仰、坚持讲法轮功真相，被中共当局多次骚扰、抓捕。每次抓捕都没有出示任何法律手续，比如搜查证等，完全是非法抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，在不通知任何亲属，法庭上只有陪送王卫真的儿子一人在场的情况下，中山区法院对她进行开庭审判。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，中山法院判王卫真<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年徒刑。后身体原因未入监。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，大连市中山区秀月派出所警察到家中抓捕了当时六十八岁的王卫真女士，将她强行劫持到大连市姚家看守所。人被送入看守所体检时，血压高至二百三十，但看守所仍然非法关押王卫真。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，王卫真女士被押辽宁女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk165272513;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159649535;"><b _Hlk159649535;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">：女，广东揭阳法轮功学员。一九七七年二月出生，揭阳市农科所法轮功学员。因张贴真相粘贴，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被榕城区公安分局警察抓捕，关押到揭阳市看守所。吴玉娟未修炼法轮功的丈夫也被拘禁了十天。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，她被揭东区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金五万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。刑期至：<span text1;">河北省石家庄市深泽县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁。家住石家庄市深泽县留村乡李家庄村，她于<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，袁文格被深泽县公安局白庄乡派出所警察从家中抓捕，关押到石家庄市第二看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日获悉：袁文格已被石家庄晋州市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，烟台市莱山区公安局有预谋的绑架了十几名法轮功学员，关押在烟台市福山看守所。其中张美玲、孙鼎美遭受八个月的关押、构陷后，被判刑，张美玲被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元；孙鼎美<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初宣判后，张美玲、孙鼎美上诉烟台市中级法院。烟台市中级法院二审维持原判。张美玲刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、张宪：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">河北香河县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生，原香河县公安局刑警队警察。自中共迫害法轮功后，张宪遭严重迫害：被开除公职，被逼流离失所，四次被劫持到洗脑班迫害，三次被非法劳教，期间惨遭酷刑折磨。张宪、王志山两位法轮功学员在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日见面时被香河县政保大队警察及派出所警察抓捕，被关押在香河县看守所，十月被批捕。于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月两人被取保候审。后于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被香河县法院判刑，张宪被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王志山遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，张宪、王志山被派出所警察又关押到香河县看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167929814;"><span lang="EN-US">2</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日因江贤俊宣讲法轮功，被一名小学生举报。随即江贤俊被警察抓捕、抄家。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉，关押在当地看守所。在其被关押、构陷一年多后，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被开庭，近悉其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日转监四川省成都市龙泉女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1960</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年代出生，河南省义马市人，六四亲历者，《零八宪章》第<span lang="EN-US">10</span>批签署人，原“温馨小屋”群主，社会时政关注者，民主异见人士，政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年，曾因参与年天安门民主运动并亲历“六四惨案”，遂自此改变了人生轨迹，坚定的走上一条中国民主运动不归路；曾因以民主推手、民权精英、博客骑士自许，而创建“温馨小屋”博客群，并在其努力经营下，使该博客群的点击量高达<span lang="EN-US">70</span>万人次；也正是因其频发民主信息和对中共当局不利的时政批评性信息，故而引起河南省当局的极度不悦与伺机打击；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，因其在微信群里传播“未经官方证实的海外消息，并对党和国家领导人有侮辱性言论”，遂被河南省义马市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又被义马市检察院以同罪名正式批捕。曹培植于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。此前被羁押于河南省渑池县看守所，后转监到河南省开封第一监狱<span lang="EN-US">15</span>监区（开封市龙亭区金耀路西环路口向西<span lang="EN-US">200</span>米路北）。已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk186442479"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">董郁玉</span></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">4</span></u></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月：</span></u></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">张忠顺、</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">2</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">宋泽、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk186352041"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">董郁玉</span></b></a></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1962</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年出生，辽宁省抚顺市人，六四亲历者，前美国哈佛大学和日本庆应义塾大学、日本北海道大学访问学者，《光明日报》评论部副主任，自由派思想者，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于北京大学法律系，<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年毕业后进入《光明日报》工作；<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年，曾因参加六四抗议活动被下放一年，后又回到《光明日报》，并曾为国内历史杂志《炎黄春秋》撰文，为《纽约时报》中文网撰写过评论；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，曾因获得美国哈佛大学尼曼新闻奖学金而在该校做访问学者<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，之后也曾在日本庆应义塾大学和北海道大学担任过访问学者；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，因与一名日本外交官在北京新侨饭店共进午餐，突然被警方带走调查，该日本外交官也被带走，数小时后被释放，但其却被长期拘押，涉嫌罪名不清；当日，日本政府对此事立即提出抗议，而中方政府则响应称，因其二人从事了与他们工作“不一致”的活动，故而被调查、拘捕；其被拘押长达一年多之后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其家属终于接到北京警方通知，声称其被以涉嫌“间谍罪”正式逮捕，并被北京市某检察院起诉；之后其案很快被移交至北京市一家法院审理；其家属坚称其既非间谍，也又非外国特工，为讨公道，此前一直选择沉默的家属决定公开此事；据悉，自其被拘押以来，其家属一直不准与其见面，代理律师也仅与其会见一次；迄今，尚不明晰法院对其审判的具体日期。目前被羁押于北京市南部某看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，董郁玉被中共当局以“间谍罪”判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/7.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/7.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">张忠顺：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1967</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日生，山东省蓬莱市人，人权捍卫者、复旦大学<span lang="EN-US">-</span>香港大学<span lang="EN-US">IMBA</span>毕业，烟台大学前教师，独立思想者，“<span lang="EN-US">12</span>·<span lang="EN-US">13</span>厦门聚会案”当事人。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年在烟台大学经济与工商管理学院任教期间，因在课堂上讲授《公共伦理学》时引用<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年六四事件视频，被学生家长举报，当年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被山东省烟台市莱山区警方秘密抓捕，家被查抄，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，并被送至济南武警总医院（济南新康监狱）关押；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”逮捕，关押于烟台市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被烟台市莱山区法院以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；上诉后烟台市中级法院二审维持原判，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被送山东省监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月出狱，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月即被烟台大学开除公职，所住房子被强拆。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月上旬，许志永、丁家喜等<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余名维权律师和人权捍卫者在厦门聚会，张忠顺是参加者之一。为此，他于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被中共当局“<span lang="EN-US">12.13</span>专案组”以“颠覆国家政权”为名监视居住，近半年后获释。此后，因为给许志永、丁家喜的辩护律师出具证言，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张忠顺第二次被山东烟台警方以同案同罪名监视居住，其住所再次遭到搜查。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，张忠顺被转押到山东临沂市临沭县看守所刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被临沂中级法院秘密开庭审理，法院事前未通知家属。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被山东临沂中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”“私藏枪支弹药罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/46_30.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/11/46_30.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">宋泽：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk159665615;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">本名宋光强，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年生，湖北襄阳人，自称襄阳宋泽。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>毕业于中南财经政法大学，法学、经济学双学士，新公民运动的参与者、倡导者。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年大学毕业后，宋泽曾在一家德资电梯企业武汉的办事处做商务行政事务工作，后又在深圳一家私营评估企业总经理办公室从事助理。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，宋泽向许志永写信，申请加入公盟，随后以志愿者的身份工作。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年冬宋泽一直在从事救助访民的工作，给访民捐助物资补给援助，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年开始了披露和救助被北京黑监狱关押的访民，维权人士。并在两会前期编绘了北京黑监狱地图。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日宋泽因给访民送汤圆而被警方带走，后不久被放出。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，宋泽与赵振甲等十多人冲进湖南郴州驻京办的「黑监狱」，解救出被非法关押的<span lang="EN-US">82</span>岁的龚江保、<span lang="EN-US">73</span>岁的于洪和<span lang="EN-US">57</span>岁的陈碧香等三位上访人士。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点宋泽在北京南站等候一位求助者的约见时，被北京公安数位警察强制带走，据宋泽本人描述应该是北京市公安局有预谋的计划。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，北京市公安局以「寻衅滋事罪」将宋泽刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天，羁押在丰台区看守所。但是期限满时，公安局没有放人，而是将刑拘转为「监视居住」，期限六个月，至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日到期。许志永认为宋泽被捕是因为救助被关押在黑监狱的三位老人和陈光诚的侄子陈克贵的妻子。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日身为公盟志愿者的宋泽被失踪，后来刘卫国律师偶然发现宋泽被关押在北京市公安局第三拘留所，涉嫌「聚众扰乱社会秩序」罪。宋泽在狱中被赵姓副队长国保殴打，方式为扇耳光、拳打脚踢，无任何人制止。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日宋泽的律师李金星、张磊联名向北京市检察院、最高检察院、公安部等部门提出了就北京市公安局有关警员涉嫌故意伤害、徇私枉法、虐待被监管人犯罪的控告状。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日宋泽由其舅舅到北京为其担保取保候审，在被羁押了<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月零<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天后，走出了北京市第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日焦作访民张小玉、许有臣案发生，为了查明真相和声援弱势群体，宋泽等人发起了公民声援团，宋泽提供账户，为张小玉案进行募捐。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日北京警方对道衡律师事务所进行抄家，将余文生律师、王成律师、宋泽、李对龙律师四人抓走。王成律师、李对龙律师不久获释。余文生律师和宋泽遭刑事拘留<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日宋泽被以取保候审的名义获释，结束了<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个多月的羁押，宋泽在押期间一直保持零口供。宋泽于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日又被武汉市公安局以“寻衅滋事”罪名刑事拘留，现羁押于武汉市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，在宋泽被抓四个月后，律师在武汉市第二看守所会见了他，被羁押是因涉嫌寻衅滋事罪和提供侵入非法计算机信息系统程序、工具罪。案件已被移送武汉市检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日获悉，其代理律师已拿到宋泽的判决书，法院认定宋泽涉嫌提供侵入非法计算机信息系统程序、工具罪名不成立，以“寻衅滋事罪”被判入狱两年六个月，刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月起至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1/</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">王炳章：遭中共关押长达<span lang="EN-US">22</span>年的王炳章博士即将迎来<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁生日 “自由王炳章”关注组发起“全球行动 营救王炳章 ”的救援运动<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，本网获悉：遭中共关押长达<span lang="EN-US">22</span>年的王炳章博士即将迎来<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁生日，“自由王炳章”关注组发起“全球行动 营救王炳章”的救援运动。“自由<a name="_Hlk186350640">王炳章</a>”关注组（推号<span lang="EN-US">@FreeWBZofficial</span>）于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日发出呼吁书：“王炳章博士<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年被中共从越南绑架回国被判处无期徒刑并被单独关押至今已有<span lang="EN-US">22</span>年，王炳章博士将于今年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日满<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁。在他生日到来之际，您的一句问候、一张明信片、一副画都会给他送去无限的温暖与关怀，我们在此呼吁大家能以不同形式给单独监禁<span lang="EN-US">22</span>年的王炳章博士庆生。”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">此呼吁一经发出，得到全世界各地的民运组织和人权组织的广泛响应。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">王炳章先生简历：</span></b></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1947</span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，河北省石家庄市籍人，基督徒，美国永久居民，民主异见人士，中国民联创始人，中国民主正义党发言人、中国民主党海外联合总部顾问，民间誉为“中国海外民主运动第一人”，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年曾在美国创办《中国之春》杂志，是中国民联的创始人，被捕前任中国民主正义党发言人、中国民主党海外联合总部顾问；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被不明身份的人在越南绑架后带到中国境内被警方拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被以“间谍和组织领导恐怖组织罪”被刑无期徒刑；据悉，其在狱中长期被单独关押，身体受到极大迫害，期间大中风一次，小中风两次，并患上严重的过敏症，病发时气喘，过敏性鼻炎，喷嚏咳嗽打个不停，使肺部、胸腔受到很大伤害，常感生不如死，冬天则是长冻疮，褥疮，薄薄一堵墙，难御严寒；其多次要求换监均不允许，其家属数年要求探监，也被拒绝，直至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其弟王炳武才被准予代表家属与其会面<span lang="EN-US">10</span>分种，并得知其一直被单独关押在狱中小号里，既不知外界任何信息，也不能有任何书信往来；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其身体可能随出现生命危险，狱方已在其囚室安放了警报器，称其一旦感到有不适即马上警报<span lang="EN-US">; 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，加拿大感恩节期间，其在加拿大生活的胞弟终于收到中国大陆狱方获准会见通知书，称此应表明其兄还活着<span lang="EN-US">; 2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，总部设在美国首都华盛顿的国际人权组织自由之家（<span lang="EN-US">Freedom House</span>）为其颁发了<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年度自由奖，以表达其对中国民主及自由所做出的努力和牺牲。目前在广东省韶关市北江监狱（广东省韶关市浈江区梨市镇<span lang="EN-US">7</span>号信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">512140</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span></span></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/2276.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/2276.html</span></b></span></span></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk170538828;"></span><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">2/</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">丁家喜：获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年的中国著名人权律师丁家喜律师的打亲情电话的权利一直被剥夺<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，本网获悉获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年的中国著名人权律师丁家喜律师打亲情电话的权利一直被剥夺。丁家喜律师妻子罗胜春日前通报：“已经五年没听到家喜的声音了，中国时间今天（<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日）上午打通了监狱狱政科电话，强烈要求保障丁家喜给我打亲情电话的权利。监狱这次的借口是无法确认我的身份，我说我是美国公民，可以把身份证明送到中国驻美大使馆请他们确认。我告诉监狱：我绝不放弃属于我的权利！”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">丁家喜简历：</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1967</span></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日出生，湖北省宜昌市人，前沈阳航空工业总公司、北京航空工业总公司工程师，曾任职北京律师协会企业重组专业委员会委员，中国民主同盟中央法制委员会委员，北航创业家协会秘书长，中关村国际孵化软件协会法律委员会主任等，原德鸿律师事务所主任，著名人权律师，北京新公民运动的组织者和协调人之一，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起，曾因积极参与推动“随迁子女就地高考”的教育平权活动，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，又与许志永、孙含会、王永红等人发表致新任中共中央总书记习近平等中共高层领导人公开信，要求包括习近平在内的<span lang="EN-US">205</span>名中国部级以上官员率先财产公示，并广泛征集公民联署超过八千余人。这些活动触动了中共脆弱敏感的神经，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被北京警方以“非法集会”罪刑事拘留，关押于北京市第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，北京警方又先后将其罪名改换为“寻衅滋事罪”和“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被北京当局以“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”开庭审案，但鉴于法院在审判中出现严重违法现象，对案件结果明显不利，故其不得不当庭宣布解除对辩护律师的委托，迫使法院只得宣布休庭，择日宣判；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，经北京市海淀区法院再次重审，终被以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后送往天津市茶淀站前进监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，又因参加一次有多名各地异见人士在福建省厦门市举办的私人聚会（后被当局称为“厦门聚会案”），同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，遂被山东警方从友人家中带走，后被烟台市警方以“厦门聚会案”主犯指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，又被临沂市临沭县警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，其案被临沂市检察院以颠覆国家政权罪名提起公诉，并移送至临沂市中级法院审判；据悉，密押期间，曾惨遭酷刑折磨，如连续<span lang="EN-US">73 </span>天被剥夺睡眠、连续<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天被“坐老虎凳”（一种极端酷刑）、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月受只有噪音和<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时照射日光灯虐待、长期不让洗澡和刷牙、甚至用餐权被剥夺等。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被中共当局判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。此前被羁押于山东省临沭县看守所。其不服上诉，二审遭驳回，维持原判。现已转监至湖北江北监狱。江北监狱位于湖北省荆州市江陵县江北大道<span lang="EN-US">228</span>号 邮编<span lang="EN-US">434110 </span>电话<span lang="EN-US">0716-4781198</span>。<span _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk183794101;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family:
