_Hlk183794101;"></span><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">3/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk186350786"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">史庭福</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">：因帮助新疆阿克苏生产建设兵团果农维权而被跨省抓捕获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年的南京人权捍卫者史庭福先生已被移送新疆兵团第一师沙河监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，本网获悉：因帮助新疆阿克苏生产建设兵团果农维权而被跨省抓捕获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年的南京人权捍卫者史庭福先生已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被移送新疆兵团第一师沙河监狱服刑。南京人权捍卫者、基督徒史庭福先生因帮助新疆阿克苏生产建设兵团果农维权，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被阿拉尔市城区公安局抓捕，随即被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日史庭福被正式批捕。此时史庭福被羁押在新疆阿克苏地区阿拉尔市看守所。后史庭福先生获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被移送新疆兵团第一师沙河监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">史庭福简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">原是南京一位争取私权利的普通访民，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁。他是一位在恶劣的环境下一步步成长为热心的维权人士，具有令中共当局恐惧的公民意识，认同三民主义与普世价值观，更是属于街头行动派的一员。他曾在南京中山陵当众喊话到访的原国民党主席的洪秀柱，希望国民党坚守民主理念；也曾现场关注南京维权人士王健被构陷案；更在苏州“<span lang="EN-US">4.29</span>”祭奠林昭时被带走。多年来，除身体力行外，史庭福先生还在网络上声援郭飞雄，为困境中的人权律师发声，在自己经济条件非常困难情况下，还资助其他更困难的维权路上的同道。此前，史庭福<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年因宣讲六四真相而被控“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕案<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日在南京法庭判史庭福犯寻衅滋事罪，处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午，史庭福先生出狱。史庭福先生出狱后因帮助新疆阿克苏生产建设兵团果农维权，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被阿拉尔市城区公安局抓捕，随即被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日史庭福被正式批捕。史庭福现被羁押在新疆阿克苏地区阿拉尔市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日获悉：史庭福先生被以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。据悉史庭福目前患有高血压、肺炎、哮喘病，身体一直不好，其被新疆警方跨省抓捕，境况令人担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。史庭福已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日移送新疆兵团第一师沙河监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/3_16.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/3_16.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">4/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">阮晓寰：一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的网络工程师阮晓寰（编程随想）案二审维持原判<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，本网获悉：一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的网络</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">工程师阮晓寰（编程随想）案于昨天<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日五下午<span lang="EN-US">2:00</span>在上海高院二审宣判，二审维持了对阮晓寰先生<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑的判决。阮晓寰妻子昨日通报：“今天下午<span lang="EN-US">14:00</span>，上海高院开庭宣判。审判长周欣，审判员：凌莉、须梅华。宣读了几段话，<span lang="EN-US">14:07</span>左右就结束了，维持原判。上海司法的一个浓臭脏印。我们会继续申诉。任何时代、任何情况，都不能让自己失去希望！出庭时阮晓寰精神状况很好。二审后家属就可以会见了……”被人誉为“用技术对抗极权的英雄”阮晓寰，曾经是上海某技术公司高管，担任过<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年北京奥运会的信息安全系统总工程师。从<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年开始，他在开通博客，取名“编程随想”，向中国网友普及翻墙技术知识和其它信息安全知识，还撰写许多有关政治、历史的文章，推荐大量“反洗脑”书籍。有无数网友因此受益，甚至受到启蒙。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">匿名撰写“编程随想”博客十二年后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，阮晓寰在家中被上海警方抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，上海法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪 ”判他有期徒刑七年，剥夺政治权利两年，罚款两万元。二审被中共当局刻意拖延，从<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日立案拖延至今。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">阮晓寰简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">网名“编程随想”。<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，福建省泉州市人，上海市杨浦区民京路<span lang="EN-US">558</span>号长住居民，网络安全工程师，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月间，曾因撰写含有针对中共当局及其政体制度等不利信息的文章百余篇，并将其发布于境外网络平台，在引发网民广泛热议的同时；也引起了中共官方的高度警惕、极端不满和伺机打击；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因其曾经常使用网名“编程随想”，被中共国安人员查出其在豆瓣网注册过用的个人信息（内含大量针对中共政权的批评性言论），遂被上海市杨浦区警方从家中带走，次日即被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，家遭查抄，当场搜走正在使用中的计算机、手机及多部<span lang="EN-US">/</span>件私人电子设备等物品；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被上海市杨浦区检察院以同罪名正式批捕，指控其因长期存有对中共政权的不满情绪，多次“使用计算机编写<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多篇带有造谣、诽谤煽颠性文章，内容涉及攻击抹黑现行政治体制、煽动颠覆国家政权、意图推翻社会主义制度”，并通过境外网站进行发布，造成大量网民浏览、评论、转发和效仿等“恶劣后果”，因而触犯了国家相关法律，应当逮捕法办；在被严重超押近<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，终被上海市第二中级法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，没收财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日；其不服，上诉；二审维持原判。据悉，其被宣判后，其父兄两家均遭警方约谈施压，“劝”其听任政府为其聘用律师，其妻亦遭警察围堵训诫<span lang="EN-US">2</span>小时；截至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，同月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日其案已被上海市高级法院立案，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，鉴于上海高级法院率先在二审期间使用“法援”律师侵占辩护席位，导致其妻委托律师无法行使合法辩护权，故其家人对相关司法人员的渎职行为和侵犯被告人辩护权等要求彻查纠正。目前阮晓寰被羁押于上海市杨浦区看守所（上海市杨浦区中原路<span lang="EN-US">1101</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">200438</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/7_14.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">5/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">张文鹏：因代理海韵集团案遭抓捕青年人权律师张文鹏狱中遭酷刑虐待<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，本网获悉：被海南警方抓捕的青年人权律师张文鹏律师的代理律师李国蓓律师昨天会见了张文鹏。张文鹏说：“每次律师会见，管教都会在门外偷听，并将偷听的话报告给侦查机关。”李国蓓律师通报：十几斤重的脚镣，从<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>号开始，三亚市第二看守所给张文鹏持续戴了<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天<span lang="EN-US">7</span>夜，至今未去除，脚踝多处磨破，伤口溃烂，期间张文鹏多次要求见驻所检，一直没来！经交涉，今天要求所领导拍照取证，明天去检察院，控告！之前一溜控告还没完，继续控告！驻所检长期不在岗找不到人玩忽职守，已经多次提出控告，死不悔改！”<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日张文鹏律师因为代理海韵集团案帮助当事人喊冤被海南三亚警方以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪予以刑事拘留。后被批捕，目前羁押于三亚第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">张文鹏简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1993</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">23</span>岁大学毕业后，张文鹏就考取得律师资格证书，按照中国的法律规定，实习一年就能获得律师执业证书，但是他实习<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年了，一直无法获得执业证。原因是他一直在反对“官办律师协会”，上了司法部的黑名单，因此青岛市司法局一直刁难他，不给他执业证，一拖就是<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。张文鹏被律师界誉为著名实习律师的一条，他揭露律协的腐败，痛斥行贿律师，因此也得罪了一些既得利益者，以至于永久被禁止执业。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年张文鹏在网上发布了实名举报信，指控青岛司法局局长万振东行贿、挥霍公款、渎职等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>大罪责。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，在山东晓临律师事务所实习的张文鹏在微博发文称：<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，他在深圳被青岛市公安局市南分局跨省传唤，他被衣服扒光，内裤都不让穿，持续传唤八小时，理由是扰乱单位秩序。张文鹏到深圳本地派出所询问，了解到，跨省传唤的事由是“曾擅自闯入了青岛司法局”。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张文鹏又因为代理海韵集团案件，帮助当事人喊冤，被三亚警方以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪予以刑事拘留。就在他被刑事拘留前，该案辩护人北大博士张庆方律师被通知将吊销律师执照。这显然就是三亚警方利用公权对海韵代理人予以打击报复。张文鹏律师后被批捕，目前羁押于三亚第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/20241213.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/20241213.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">6/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">黎智英：香港《苹果日报》、壹传媒创办人黎智英在狱中度过其<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁生日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，本网获悉<span lang="EN-US">: 12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日是香港《苹果日报》、壹传媒创办人黎智英先生的生日，黎智英先生在狱中度过了其<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁生日。黎智英曾在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8.18</span>维园“六四集会案”及<span lang="EN-US">8.31</span>“港岛游行案”被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月和<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，又被香港西九龙法院就其<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年“港岛游行案”和<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年“六四集会案”数次庭审宣判，刑期共计<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，香港当局再次对支持民主人权的香港《苹果日报》、壹传媒创办人黎智英判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。最后所谓“勾结外国势力危害国家安全罪”正在审理。香港当局正在依照中共当局的意图欲置<span lang="EN-US">77</span>岁的黎智英先生于死地。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">黎智英简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1947</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，英文名<span lang="EN-US">Jimmy Lai Chee-ying</span>，生于中国广州市，祖籍广东省顺德市，现为香港永久性居民，佐丹奴（<span lang="EN-US">Giordano</span>）集团公司老板，香港《苹果日报》、壹传媒及《壹周刊》创办人，香港知名商人，香港民主派政党及组织的重要资助者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年，曾因生活穷困而被迫随广东发生的大规模“逃港潮”，借道澳门逃亡香港谋生，后经努力拼搏，于<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年创办了连锁服装品牌佐丹奴（<span lang="EN-US">Giordano</span>），并迅速使之成为当时风靡中港台的主要时装品牌之一；<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年，曾因同情天安门民主运动中的抗议学生，其旗下的佐丹奴印制了大量印有民运口号的<span lang="EN-US">T</span>恤供人们游行抗议时穿着，其本人也发表公开信敦促时任中国总理的李鹏下台谢罪，遂遭到六四镇压之后北京对香港商人的首批整肃，佐丹奴集团公司在中国大陆的全部业务被当局封杀，致其公司损失惨重，被迫低价出售股权；自此，其弃商从文，转而投身传媒事业，先后创办了壹传媒、《壹周刊》和《苹果日报》，但又因时常抨击中共时弊而被中国大陆禁止入境，其经手的报刊书籍亦被列入黑名单；长期以来，曾因其是香港民主运动（如香港雨伞运动、香港“反送中”抗议活动等）的重要支持者和资助商，故备受北京当局及香港建制派的批评、斥责，甚至指控其捐款为黑金；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因与美国副总统彭斯及美国国务卿蓬佩奥委会面，谈及香港现状及未来前途等事宜，而遭到中共当局的极度仇视和要打击的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被香港警方以涉嫌“非法集结罪”抓捕，后被释放；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，又被以触犯香港《国安法》，涉嫌“勾结外国或者境外势力危害国家安全罪”及“串谋欺诈及煽动罪”拘捕，后暂获保释；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又被指控“欺诈罪”而收监逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天后，再被加控“勾结外国或者境外势力危害国家安全罪”被庭审；后其虽暂获保释，但<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日再度被捕，关押于香港荔枝角收押所，后与同案民主派高层领袖李卓人被香港西九龙裁判法院就<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8.18</span>维园“六四集会案”及<span lang="EN-US">8.31</span>“港岛游行案”进行宣判，其二人同时被判刑期<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；之后很快其持有的壹传媒公司股份（市值超过<span lang="EN-US">3</span>亿元港币）及对其他三家公司在香港银行账户内所拥有的财产均被香港国安局冻结；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月和<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，又被香港西九龙法院就其<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年“港岛游行案”和<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年“六四集会案”数次庭审宣判，刑期共计<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，再被以其名下的力高公司涉嫌违反与特区政府香港科技园公司订立的地契为由，被特区高等法院以“欺诈罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">200</span>万港元（<span lang="EN-US">25.69</span>万美元<span lang="EN-US">/179</span>万元人民币），取消担任公司董事资格<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年；另有“勾结外国势力危害国家安全罪”案仍在审理。目前在香港赤柱监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/77.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/77.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">7/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">张春雷：一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年的贵阳仁爱归正教会张春雷长老案二审维持原判<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，本网获悉：贵阳仁爱归正教会张春雷长老被控“煽动颠覆国家政权罪、诈骗罪”一案于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在贵州省贵阳市中级人民法院进行宣判，张春雷长老被判处煽动颠覆国家政权罪三年六个月，诈骗罪两年，合并执行五年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日止。张春雷长老不服一审判决，依法上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日贵州省高院维持了贵阳市中院以煽颠罪和诈骗罪名义对张春雷长老五年有期徒刑的判决。张春雷长老已被羁押三年九个月，其患有肝硬化等疾病，家属对此非常担忧。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">张春雷简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1964</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生<span lang="EN-US">, </span>贵州省人，基督徒，贵阳市仁爱归正家庭教会主要组建人，教会带领人、长老，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年《牧者联署：为基督信仰的声明》首批签名人之一，中国在押良心犯。早年，曾因笃信耶稣基督，为广传基督教福音而与人共同组建了不从中共“三自教会”的“仁爱归正教会”；起初，该教会仅有几十会众，但在其不懈努力和事工（即神职人员在教会里所做的服务）带领下，因能热情广泛接待南来北往的信徒，故而在后来的国度事工中起到和发挥了重要的作用；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，曾因积极参与由四川成都王怡牧师发起的《牧者联署：为基督信仰的声明》的首批联署签名，随遭贵阳当局的严管监控；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其教会被贵阳市南明区民族宗教事务局突然取缔，并被指称，因其等一行人“未经批准，擅自以‘仁爱归正教会’名义在南明区中天商务港设立宗教场所，组织、举行宗教活动，接受宗教性捐献，违反《宗教事务条例》相关规定，责令停止宗教活动，拆除相关设施和标识”，最终致使其及教会信徒在失去会堂后只能在餐厅、酒店进行主日敬拜；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因在当地某酒店举行主日聚会，而被数十名宗教局人员及警方先后<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次连手冲击，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次被封门，敬拜所用的十字架被强摘，其计算机等用品被查收；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因其教会新租房屋的房东再次被当局威胁，故而其被逼无奈只得再次从新租的房屋搬走；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其教会有十数名信众在参加小组学习时被突然闯入的贵阳市南明区民宗局人员和警方带走，遂其赶到派出所与警方交涉要人，不料竟遭粗暴野蛮对待，并被以“非法经营社团”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">11</span>天；拘留期满时，又被贵阳市云岩区警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被贵阳市云岩区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；据悉，其妻子、儿子受牵连曾遭警方长时讯问且其妻遭虐待，教会多位同工成员亦遭抄家；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其代理律师数次要求会见均受阻，被告知其“因涉嫌危害国家安全，在侦查期间未得到办案单位允许的情况下，禁止律师会见”。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年初遭起诉。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日开庭，未宣判张春雷长老被控“煽动颠覆国家政权罪、诈骗罪”一案于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">10:00</span>在贵州省贵阳市中级人民法院进行宣判，张春雷长被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。目前张春雷长老被羁押于贵阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/5.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/5.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">8/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">黄琦：获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年的著名人权捍卫者<a name="_Hlk186353813">黄琦</a>入狱已经整整八年<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年的著名人权捍卫者、六四天网创办人、年已<span lang="EN-US">61</span>岁的黄琦先生入狱已经整整八年。黄琦因从事人权事业多次被捕入狱，三次被判刑，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年因为弱势群体维权，呼吁保护人权，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年因曝光豆腐渣工程致死学生，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日再遭抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。其坐牢<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，母亲蒲文清也已<span lang="EN-US">90</span>多岁，身体状况持续恶化，母子俩的会见权利没有得到任何保障。其母亲仍然处于<span lang="EN-US"> 24 </span>小时监控之中。而黄琦有肾功能衰竭、冠心病、脑积水等多种严重疾病，维权网敦促中国政府从人道主义出发，允许黄琦保外就医。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">黄琦简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1963</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，四川省内江市人“六四天网”网站创办人、中国天网人权事务中心负责人，人权捍卫者，中国在押良心犯。因长期关注社会热点话题，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年曾成立“天网寻人事务所”，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年曾设立“六四天网”网站，并惯于在网上发表时政敏感性文章，从而累遭当局严控、传唤、刑拘和判刑；曾因言获罪，先后三次遭到警方的拘捕，且前两次都被判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，曾因国外异议人士在其网页上发表有关<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年天安门事件的文章，而被四川成都警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被四川省成都市中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；狱中曾遭法警、狱警和其他罪犯多次毒打，导致脑积水，脑萎缩，双侧脑室扩大，导水管变窄等严重疾病；出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，曾改组六四天网为中国天网人权事务中心，创办了中国大陆第一家综合性人权组织，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日荣获第六届中国人权青年奖；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，曾因发表有关四川地震灾难问政府的报导（即网上发文揭露汶川地震出现的“豆腐渣”工程），而第二次被成都市警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被正式逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被成都市武侯区法院以“非法持有国家秘密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US"> 2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日刑满释放；然而此时因在狱中长期遭受煎熬和非人待遇，已罹患肾脏绝症；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因对一份内部文件内容曝光，其第三次被四川省绵阳市警方从成都家中带走刑事拘留，自此失联，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被以“为境外非法泄露国家机密罪”正式逮捕，并被关押在绵阳看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，其案被移交四川绵阳市法院审理；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被四川省绵阳市法院一审以“故意泄露国家秘密罪”、“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”共判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年；其不服上诉，后经绵阳市中级人民法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。目前被在四川省巴中监狱服刑。据悉，黄琦狱中曾遭虐待迫害，常被犯人殴打致腿部受伤，家人所寄存款亦被狱警随意扣押；身体健康极差，有肾功能衰竭危险，患脑积水、心脏病、肺气肿和肺炎等多种严重疾患。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/12.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/12.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">9/</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">黄晓敏：获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的四川民主维权人士黄晓敏狱中患病 身体状况堪忧<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，本网获悉：四川民主维权人士黄晓敏于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被成都市警方莫名以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，后被转逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉，近期已被成都市金牛区法院以同罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。日前，本网据知情人士透露，黄晓敏狱中患肺病，身体状况堪忧。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">黄晓敏简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1962</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，网名“牛鬼的儿子”，河南省新野县籍人，前新疆喀什市疏勒县农三师党校教师，六四民运参与者，自由撰稿人，独立中文笔会会员，四川泛蓝联盟召集人，民主维权人士，中国在押政治犯。早年曾生长于新疆喀什市农三师伽师总厂，后从喀什农学院农学系毕业，就职于新疆喀什农三师党校任教师；<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年辞职后，前往四川省成都市居住至今，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月成为独立中文笔会会员；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，曾因现场采访鲍俊生等上访人员在四川成都中级法院大门外举行的“链子门”事件抗议示威活动，要求释放<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被捕的“六四天网”负责人黄琦等，并与友人共同拍录像像，发往海内外媒体刊登，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被成都市金牛区警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”抓捕、刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被正式逮捕，并被关押于乐山市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被乐山市市中区法院一审以同罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，二审依然维持原判，刑至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被释放；出狱后，因继续参与维权活动，接受外媒采访，在网上发表有关民主维权文章，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-5</span>月，又因积极介入了云南省委党校退休教师子肃发表公开信要求中共<span lang="EN-US">19</span>大开放直选、选举胡德平为总书记事件，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被成都警方秘密绑架，自此失联，家被查抄；其家人为知其下落被迫做寻人启事，后得知其早已被成都警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，其案被成都市金牛区检察院起诉至金牛区法院；至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，被成都市金牛区法院以“寻衅滋事罪“判处<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月有期徒刑；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，又被成都市警方莫名以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，后被转逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉，近期已被成都市金牛区法院以同罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。此前被羁押于成都市看守所，后转监至四川成都市锦江监狱（成都市高新区中和街道迎江路<span lang="EN-US">9</span>号）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/4.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/4.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">10/</span></b></span></span></span><a name="_Hlk186442143"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">全世欣</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">：获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月的北京维权人士全世欣女士已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日转到天河监狱服刑<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 楷体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">（维权网信息中心报道）<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，本网获悉：获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月的北京维权人士全世欣女士已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日转到天河监狱服刑。全世欣女士于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月因接受美国之音采访，被刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。后全世欣女士一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，二审维持原判。此前全世欣被羁押于北京市海淀区看守所，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。全世欣女士<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日就两会被维稳监控接受了美国之音采访，随即遭抓捕，其推特账号停留在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。过去的一年多，全世欣的法律权利全部被剥夺，她現在拒絕了官方指定律師，当局又不讓她自己聘請律師，沒有直系親屬在外面幫她聘請律師，所以到現在沒有其认可的律師。全世欣女士要求当局保障其自行委托辩护律师的权利，保障会见驻看守所的检察官的权利，后其毅然绝食抗议，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被强行灌食。后再遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">全世欣简历：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，北京市人，北京市海淀区四季青东平庄<span lang="EN-US">56</span>号居民，维权人士，贪腐举报人，网络推友。早年曾因个人宅基地及住房被政府强拆而被迫维权多年，至今仍未获批宅基地或获赔住房，成为无家可归的北京土著农民；在维权过程中，因发现地方干部有严重贪腐现象，并公开向多个职能部门举报，随遭地方当权者严厉打压和非法拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，因使用互联网翻墙软件在推特上发表对中共当局及执政者批评言论，被网警监控发现，而被北京海淀区警方因言获罪，立刻以“寻衅滋事”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又因身穿写有“蔡奇见家属”字样的白色短袖<span lang="EN-US">T</span>恤，高喊要求与市政府相关负责人见面递交相关材料，寻求解决问题，而被海淀区警方以“扰乱公共场所秩序”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，再次被海淀区警方莫名带走，后被以“寻衅滋事”罪由刑拘，好友疑称此与其曾在推特上多次发支持香港“反送中”抗议游行等言论有关；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其被北京市海淀区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其被起诉，起诉书称其“自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年注册并使用推特，散布大量虚假信息，严重扰乱社会秩序”，因而触犯刑法，需要提交法院予以审判；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其案在北京市海淀区法院开庭受理，后又长期休庭；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，终被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，刑满释放。此前被羁押于北京市海淀区看守所。全世欣女士<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日就两会被维稳监控接受了美国之音采访，随即遭抓捕，其推特账号停留在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。后被刑事拘留、批捕，已被检察院起诉，建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。其身患心脏病，现在又绝食抗争，其狱中健康令人担忧。最后全世欣女士一审获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，二审维持原判。全世欣女士此前被羁押于北京市海淀区看守所，已于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日转到天河监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/2920241224.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/2920241224.html</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175883967;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk167930243"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">四、</span></b></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">本期新增被刑事拘留、被精神病、强迫失踪的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人名单及简历<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">：</span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><a name="_Hlk175805580"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">李宜雪、多杰旦仁、刘汉斌、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></a></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175805580;"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk175805580;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">李宜雪：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">江西维权人士<a name="_Hlk186345970">，女。</a>李宜雪女士维权事件源于其在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日遭派出所辅警猥亵，并在向警方指控后，竟然被警方送至江西省精神病院强制入院<span lang="EN-US">56</span>日的事件。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，南昌市公安局西湖分局发通报回应，认定涉事辅警赖某吉不存在猥亵行为，并指李宜雪在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月中先后<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次在公共场合扬言自杀、自称患有抑郁症、难以入睡，丁公路派出所因此将其送至江西省精神病院，医院诊断后收治入院，民警也于当日通知家属。李宜雪后以医疗损害责任纠纷为由起诉江西省精神病院，并在网上曝光遭遇、发视频回应通报。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，诉江西省精神病院案一审开庭，庭审约两个小时，法院宣布择期宣判。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，李宜雪发布两则短视频称西湖分局筷子巷派出所所长带十余人闯入家中并破坏门口监控设备，此后李宜雪失联，引发网民持续关注。西湖区委宣传部<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日通报称，当地小区此后每日上门关心，李宜雪一直在家中。大批中国大陆网民尝试多种方式联系李宜雪未果。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，南昌市公安局西湖分局、西湖区南浦街道办事处发布通告称，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日夜间北京安定医院<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名专家（另<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名民警、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>名小区干部陪同）已在协商后上门到李宜雪家中为李宜雪鉴定，并与李宜雪父亲谈话，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日北京安定医院作出李宜雪患有强迫性障碍、人格障碍，鉴于李宜雪当前病情，<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日已将其送诊。上述公告并未打消公众质疑，相反，大陆民间舆论对中共当局再次强制将李宜雪关进精神病院一事表达强烈的不满，谴责之声一夜之间如海啸一般。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/blog-post_23.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: text1;">2</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="color: black; style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">藏族，他是位于青海果洛州久治县的多杰旦民族职业技术学校校长<a name="_Hlk186346607">。多杰旦仁</a>波切于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月初被失踪，中共当局警告当地僧俗民众不得谈论他被失踪情况和传送他的开示视频等。多杰旦职业学校有<span lang="EN-US">1300</span>多学生，藏人开始担心这个职校的命运。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/blog-post_81.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: text1;">3</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><b><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、刘汉斌：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">重庆自媒体人，网名：文艺犯。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，刘汉斌因公开声援内蒙古清河县失地农民维权，被内蒙古呼和浩特警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”跨省抓捕，并被刑事拘留，目前关押在呼和浩特市第一看守所。律师提出取保候审的请求，于<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被呼和浩特警方以“案件重大复杂”为由拒绝，并且限制律师的正常会见权利。刘汉斌是一名长期关注社会问题、敢于揭露真相的自媒体人。他通过个人平台记录和揭露中国基层社会的不公现象，特别是失地农民的困境。此次事件的起因是刘汉斌公开支持内蒙古清河县失地农民的维权行动，揭露当地政府强行征地、补偿不足等问题。这些失地农民多年来上访未果，甚至遭到地方政府的暴力打压和非法拘禁。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk167930243;"></span></span></span><a text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">杨毓萍、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">杨美华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">年：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">孙超、李俊飞、苑俊丰、</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><a name="_Hlk186343344"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">1</span></b></a></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk186343344;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、帕尔哈提·吐尔逊</span></b></span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1969</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，维吾尔族名</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-themecolor: text1;">پەرھات</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;"> </span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-themecolor: text1;">تۇرسۇن</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">，<span lang="EN-US">Perhat Tursun</span>，新疆维吾尔自治区克孜勒苏柯尔克孜自治州阿图什市人，乌鲁木齐市天山区团结路街道领馆巷北小区居住公民，原新疆维吾尔自治区群众艺术馆公职人员，著名维吾尔作家、诗人及文化评论家，因言获罪者，中国在押政治犯。早于<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代，因中国正值出版限制逐渐松绑时期，遂有包括新疆维吾尔族在内的读者群有机会开始接触西方现代文学著作，其亦在此时代氛围下在一座图书馆翻阅到一本名为《当代著名作家》的维吾尔文书籍；虽然该书仅是印有少数西方作家作品摘录的小书，但其却被书中对福克纳和叔本华的介绍及其字句所吸引，自此其对西方文化思想极有兴致；后其远赴北京中央民族大学就读，主修维吾尔文学；初入学时，除能写出自己的名字以外其汉语程度极差，但当其发现大学图书馆里竟藏有大批西方著作之汉语译本时，其开始苦练汉语，以使自己能阅读和理解更多的西方文学与哲学书籍；大学毕业后，开始在新疆乌鲁木齐市的自治区群众艺术馆服务；因其善用闲暇时间写作，并且写作重点旨在关注城市异化、维吾尔传统和人类生存问题等，遂很快着有诗集《情诗一百首》、中篇小说《弥赛亚的荒凉》、长篇小说《自杀的艺术》等作品；但因其作品有明显受西方文化思想（尤其是存在主义）色彩的影响，故让其在维吾尔社群中引起争议，成为一位集名望与争议于一身的公知人物；据悉，其曾被人扣上了「反伊斯兰」的帽子，被质疑其对自身民族的忠诚，称其思想是“民族的耻辱”，进而被跟踪、骚扰甚至收到死亡威胁；尽管其不认为自己反伊斯兰，但也不属于任何一阵营，只是喜好思考一些当时社会隐避不谈的议题（即敏感话题），故而自此再无国内出版社及媒体愿意<span lang="EN-US">/</span>敢于刊登其相关文章；尤其是<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年其出版的《自杀的艺术》，因书名涉及敏感字词，而被出版社更改译名为《毁灭的爱》，作者译名也稍有不同，并且在当下，该书已几乎从中国出版市场上绝迹，新疆人民出版社的在线书目也已找不到其任何维吾尔文的书籍信息；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，其在中央民族大学获得文学博士学位，研究方向为察合台语和维吾尔民俗学，尤其是专精于<span lang="EN-US">15</span>世纪的帖木尔帝国诗人阿里希尔·纳瓦依（<span lang="EN-US">Alishir Nava'i</span>）著作，特别是改写自阿拉伯经典故事的察合台文长诗《莱丽与麦吉侬》；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，其曾针对其的争议响应称，「我只是喜欢写，没人敢写它，所以我只是为自己而写」；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，其被中共新疆当局突然将其拘留，罪名不详，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获悉，其因被控在「民族认同的促进与表达」上存有异议（具体罪名不清），已被新疆乌鲁木齐市中级法院重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">16</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月；据知情人士称，其在被抓捕前，手边还有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>部小说正在撰写中，另有一题名《<span lang="EN-US">The Big City</span>》的小说（描绘维吾尔族学生在大城市里的疏离经验的故事）尚未出版。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/16_27.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/16_27.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178434051;"></span><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk186342950"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">2</span></b></a></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk186342950;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、任建平：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk186342950;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1964</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk186342950;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，原籍四川省绵阳市人，重庆市沙坪坝区南方香榭里小区<span lang="EN-US">22</span>号附<span lang="EN-US">2</span>号居住公民，民主人士，“推墙大联盟（<span lang="EN-US">LTDW</span>）”主要发起人，“推墙大联盟案”受害者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年底，其因致力于追求中国民主宪政之路，而与多名海内外参与者连手合作，积极筹划、组建推特群，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日将该推特群命名为“推墙大联盟（<span lang="EN-US">LTDW</span>）<span lang="EN-US">@LTDW2025</span>”，明确其宗旨是“坚守现代民主政治理念、推翻独裁专制和理性抗争原则，携手联盟共进，为实现中国的自由、民主、人权和宪政而努力”，并且“推墙”就是“推翻中国共产党的领导”；因其“推墙”理念及主张迅速得到了海内外众多推友的支持与响应，很快有<span lang="EN-US">200</span>多人参加，并迅速扩展出“民主群”、“自由群”、“<span lang="EN-US">N5</span>群”等<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余个“推墙”子群；因其与众多群友共同积极在网上参与多起维权、民主事件，传播各种人权、民主讯息，以启蒙广大民众，故而被网络上的中共水军获取，使当局对其等推出的信息与敏感信息十分紧张和恼怒，因触及到当权者的利益及其主导的专制意识形态，遂将此列为大案要案，对其等参与者进行秘查；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其在“推墙大联盟案”大抓捕中，被重庆市沙坪坝区警方从家中带走，家遭查抄，隔天即被以涉嫌“煽颠覆国家政府罪”刑拘，送重庆市沙坪坝看守所关押；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其又被警方以同罪名转为正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其及另<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名民主党被以「推墙大联盟案」共犯被当地检察院以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”提起公诉，指控其等利用网络社群媒体，大量发布危害国家安全和社会主义制度的言论，煽动民众纪念六四，炒作境内敏感热点事件，攻击中共的领导及其现行政治体制，辱骂党和国家领导人，煽动颠覆中共政权；后其等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人“颠覆罪”案被检察院移交至重庆市第一中级法院审查，并于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日开庭审理未果，后被一再延审；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案终于被重庆市第一中级法院以「颠覆国家政府罪」统一宣判，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被判<span lang="EN-US">4-10</span>不等刑期，其中，因其发起人身份而被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日；据悉，因重庆当局一直对此案严密封锁信息，恐吓家属，故使其等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被抓捕、判刑及在狱中身心健康等情况一直毫不知情。目前服刑监狱不详。</span></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk186342950;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">信息来源：</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk186342950;"></span></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/10.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk186342950;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/10.html</span></b></span></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk186342950;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;"> </span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk186342950;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk186342950;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">3</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk186342950;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-themecolor: text1;">、毛丽旦·依拉吾冬</span></b></span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">1986</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，女，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Mewlude Hilalidin</span>，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州伊宁市人，伊宁市伊犁街五巷<span lang="EN-US">33</span>号公民，土耳其公民身份持有者，语言教师，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，曾以国际留学生身分前往土耳其求学，后在土耳其伊斯坦堡大学攻读并获工商管理学位；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年底<span lang="EN-US">-2013</span>年初，其返回国内，在新疆伊宁市当地一所私立学校担任英语和土耳其语教师；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其在当年中共新疆当局开始大规模以反恐的名义大量修建或扩建再教育基地之际，因其曾到过土耳其留学，又是维吾尔族人，故被关进当地一所「再教育营」培训；后其虽于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获释，但在同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日又被伊宁市警方以涉嫌「分裂国家」罪名再次被逮捕，并被羁押至伊宁县吉里于孜镇看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其案在伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州伊宁市中级法院开庭审理，最终被以「分裂国家罪」重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日；据悉，其在土耳其求学期间，并未参与过当地的任何政治活动，但却自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年起被伊宁市警方归类为「长期逾期在外人员」和「使用快牙软件（即<span lang="EN-US">Zapya</span>，一款点对点的文件共享应用程序）人员的关系人员」。目前在新疆伊犁女子监狱（新疆伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州伊宁市飞机场东街<span lang="EN-US">212</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">835000</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，李卓忠、廖燕琼夫妇遭兴宁市公安局国保大队抓捕。随即遭刑事拘留，后遭批捕、起诉，警察将他带到兴宁市医院强制做体检，结果显示他有肺结核，被看守所拒收。其在梅州市病残收治戒毒中心关押。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，中共开始大规模迫害法轮功后，杜秀艳屡遭迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，杜秀艳再被哈尔滨市阿城区国保警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月中旬，她被阿城区法院庭审，遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，现已被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"></span></span><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/9.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/12/9.html</span></b></span></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">7</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">、邹家成：</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">1997</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><span style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-themecolor: text1;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，英文名<span lang="EN-US">Owen Chow Ka Shing</span>，中华人民共和国（香港）籍和英国籍人，香港新界东民主派初选参选人，「墨落无悔」声明书发起人之一，民主派人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因其有意参选香港该年立法会选举，曾与泛民主派人士张可森、梁晃维联合发起抗争派立场的「墨落无悔」声明书，最终成功号召了多名泛民主派有意参选人加入联署，迫使香港政府响应「五大要求」；之后，其又递交报名表参加<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-12</span>日投票的香港民主派立法会新界东初选，宣扬本土派理念，参选口号是“拒绝殖民，民族抗暴”——因其认为，虽然民主派以“<span lang="EN-US">35+</span>”为目标，但港共派手法层出不穷，故其强调无论议席最终能否过半数，都「要喊话让全世界听，我是香港民族」；期间，其亦为「<span lang="EN-US">12</span>港人案」与朱凯廸、黄之锋等人连手四处奔波，为被捕者及其家属争取应有的权利，努力让此事件被香港本地及国际社会予以关注；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，官方媒体《文汇报》明确指其为「煽暴<span lang="EN-US">'</span>素人<span lang="EN-US">'</span>（即无党籍）邹家成”，遂其自此意味着被官方视为“港独分子”；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，在香港民主派初选大搜捕中，其遭香港警务处国家安全处拘捕，并其多部电子器材、扣帐卡及信用卡被没收，其花旗银行、恒生银行及汇丰<span lang="EN-US">PayMe</span>的财务纪录获得；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其与另<span lang="EN-US">46</span>人被警方以涉嫌「串谋颠覆国家政权罪」均被起诉，且其被国安法指定法官拒绝保释，续押至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，之后获香港高等法院批准保释；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其因保释期间发送<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>贴文被认为危害国家安全及违反法庭保释条件，又被收监逮捕，续押候审；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，因其律师胡咏斯在荔枝角接待中心依法与其见面时，其将一份投诉表格交给胡律师，后被警方发现而被视为私拿“未经授权物品”，被控二人“将未经授权物品携离监狱”罪；因二人对其指控不认罪、不作供或传唤证人，最后在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被西九龙裁判法院裁定罪成，分别被判处三天监禁和罚款<span lang="EN-US">1800</span>港币；<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其因<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年参演所谓<span lang="EN-US">7.1</span>立法会暴动案而被西九龙裁判法院以「暴动罪」判囚<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，在「<span lang="EN-US">47</span>人案」中，又被西九龙裁判法院再次以「串谋颠覆国家政权罪」判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月；其等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人对定罪及刑期不服，提起上诉，但截至<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，司法机构纪录显示：案件暂未排期；因其正在就「暴动罪」服刑，刑期预至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年出狱。之前曾被押在香港赤柱监狱，目前被羁押于荔枝角收押所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk178514727;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk162448506;"><b lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，高晓颖被秦都区法院开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获悉，他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至<span _Hlk162448506;"><a name="_Hlk186351945"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: black; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New
